running;\n   109→\n   110→    /* true when the caller wants to ignore all unsent/inflight messages and force close.  */\n   111→    private volatile boolean forceClose;\n   112→\n   113→    /* metrics */\n   114→    private final SenderMetrics sensors;\n   115→\n   116→    /* the max time to wait for the server to respond to the request*/\n   117→    private final int requestTimeoutMs;\n   118→\n   119→    /* The max time to wait before retrying a request which has failed */\n   120→    private final long retryBackoffMs;\n   121→\n   122→    /* all the state related to transactions, in particular the producer id, producer epoch, and sequence numbers */\n   123→    private final TransactionManager transactionManager;\n   124→\n   125→    // A per-partition queue of batches ordered by creation time for tracking the in-flight batches\n   126→    private final Map<TopicPartition, List<ProducerBatch>> inFlightBatches;\n   127→\n   128→    public Sender(LogContext logContext,\n   129→                  KafkaClient client,\n   130→                  ProducerMetadata metadata,\n   131→                  RecordAccumulator accumulator,\n   132→                  boolean guaranteeMessageOrder,\n   133→                  int maxRequestSize,\n   134→                  short acks,\n   135→                  int retries,\n   136→                  SenderMetricsRegistry metricsRegistry,\n   137→                  Time time,\n   138→                  int requestTimeoutMs,\n   139→                  long retryBackoffMs,\n   140→                  TransactionManager transactionManager) {\n   141→        this.log = logContext.logger(Sender.class);\n   142→        this.client = client;\n   143→        this.accumulator = accumulator;\n   144→        this.metadata = metadata;\n   145→        this.guaranteeMessageOrder = guaranteeMessageOrder;\n   146→        this.maxRequestSize = maxRequestSize;\n   147→        this.running = true;\n   148→        this.acks = acks;\n   149→        this.retries = retries;\n   150→        this.time = time;\n   151→        this.sensors = new SenderMetrics(metricsRegistry, metadata, client, time);\n   152→        this.requestTimeoutMs = requestTimeoutMs;\n   153→        this.retryBackoffMs = retryBackoffMs;\n   154→        this.transactionManager = transactionManager;\n   155→        this.inFlightBatches = new HashMap<>();\n   156→    }\n   157→\n   158→    public List<ProducerBatch> inFlightBatches(TopicPartition tp) {\n   159→        return inFlightBatches.containsKey(tp) ? inFlightBatches.get(tp) : new ArrayList<>();\n   160→    }\n   161→\n   162→    private void maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(ProducerBatch batch) {\n   163→        List<ProducerBatch> batches = inFlightBatches.get(batch.topicPartition);\n   164→        if (batches != null) {\n   165→            batches.remove(batch);\n   166→            if (batches.isEmpty()) {\n   167→                inFlightBatches.remove(batch.topicPartition);\n   168→            }\n   169→        }\n   170→    }\n   171→\n   172→    private void maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(ProducerBatch batch) {\n   173→        maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\n   174→        this.accumulator.deallocate(batch);\n   175→    }\n   176→\n   177→    /**\n   178→     *  Get the in-flight batches that has reached delivery timeout.\n   179→     */\n   180→    private List<ProducerBatch> getExpiredInflightBatches(long now) {\n   181→        List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = new ArrayList<>();\n   182→\n   183→        for (Iterator<Map.Entry<TopicPartition, List<ProducerBatch>>> batchIt = inFlightBatches.entrySet().iterator(); batchIt.hasNext();) {\n   184→            Map.Entry<TopicPartition, List<ProducerBatch>> entry = batchIt.next();\n   185→            List<ProducerBatch> partitionInFlightBatches = entry.getValue();\n   186→            if (partitionInFlightBatches != null) {\n   187→                Iterator<ProducerBatch> iter = partitionInFlightBatches.iterator();\n   188→                while (iter.hasNext()) {\n   189→                    ProducerBatch batch = iter.next();\n   190→                    if (batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(accumulator.getDeliveryTimeoutMs(), now)) {\n   191→                        iter.remove();\n   192→                        // expireBatches is called in Sender.sendProducerData, before client.poll.\n   193→                        // The !batch.isDone() invariant should always hold. An IllegalStateException\n   194→                        // exception will be thrown if the invariant is violated.\n   195→                        if (!batch.isDone()) {\n   196→                            expiredBatches.add(batch);\n   197→                        } else {\n   198→                            throw new IllegalStateException(batch.topicPartition + \" batch created at \" +\n   199→                                batch.createdMs + \" gets unexpected final state \" + batch.finalState());\n   200→                        }\n   201→                    } else {\n   202→                        accumulator.maybeUpdateNextBatchExpiryTime(batch);\n   203→                        break;\n   204→                    }\n   205→                }\n   206→                if (partitionInFlightBatches.isEmpty()) {\n   207→                    batchIt.remove();\n   208→                }\n   209→            }\n   210→        }\n   211→        return expiredBatches;\n   212→    }\n   213→\n   214→    private void addToInflightBatches(List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\n   215→        for (ProducerBatch batch : batches) {\n   216→            List<ProducerBatch> inflightBatchList = inFlightBatches.computeIfAbsent(batch.topicPartition,\n   217→                k -> new ArrayList<>());\n   218→            inflightBatchList.add(batch);\n   219→        }\n   220→    }\n   221→\n   222→    public void addToInflightBatches(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches) {\n   223→        for (List<ProducerBatch> batchList : batches.values()) {\n   224→            addToInflightBatches(batchList);\n   225→        }\n   226→    }\n   227→\n   228→    private boolean hasPendingTransactionalRequests() {\n   229→        return transactionManager != null && transactionManager.hasPendingRequests() && transactionManager.hasOngoingTransaction();\n   230→    }\n   231→\n   232→    /**\n   233→     * The main run loop for the sender thread\n   234→     */\n   235→    @Override\n   236→    public void run() {\n   237→        log.debug(\"Starting Kafka producer I/O thread.\");\n   238→\n   239→        // main loop, runs until close is called\n   240→        while (running) {\n   241→            try {\n   242→                runOnce();\n   243→            } catch (Exception e) {\n   244→                log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n   245→            }\n   246→        }\n   247→\n   248→        log.debug(\"Beginning shutdown of Kafka producer I/O thread, sending remaining records.\");\n   249→\n   250→        // okay we stopped accepting requests but there may still be\n   251→        // requests in the transaction manager, accumulator or waiting for acknowledgment,\n   252→        // wait until these are completed.\n   253→        while (!forceClose && ((this.accumulator.hasUndrained() || this.client.inFlightRequestCount() > 0) || hasPendingTransactionalRequests())) {\n   254→            try {\n   255→                runOnce();\n   256→            } catch (Exception e) {\n   257→                log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n   258→            }\n   259→        }\n   260→\n   261→        // Abort the transaction if any commit or abort didn't go through the transaction manager's queue\n   262→        while (!forceClose && transactionManager != null && transactionManager.hasOngoingTransaction()) {\n   263→            if (!transactionManager.isCompleting()) {\n   264→                log.info(\"Aborting incomplete transaction due to shutdown\");\n   265→                try {\n   266→                    // It is possible for the transaction manager to throw errors when aborting. Catch these\n   267→                    // so as not to interfere with the rest of the shutdown logic.\n   268→                    transactionManager.beginAbort();\n   269→                } catch (Exception e) {\n   270→                    log.error(\"Error in kafka producer I/O thread while aborting transaction when during closing: \", e);\n   271→                    // Force close in case the transactionManager is in error states.\n   272→                    forceClose = true;\n   273→                }\n   274→            }\n   275→            try {\n   276→                runOnce();\n   277→            } catch (Exception e) {\n   278→                log.error(\"Uncaught error in kafka producer I/O thread: \", e);\n   279→            }\n   280→        }\n   281→\n   282→        if (forceClose) {\n   283→            // We need to fail all the incomplete transactional requests and batches and wake up the threads waiting on\n   284→            // the futures.\n   285→            if (transactionManager != null) {\n   286→                log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete transactional requests due to forced shutdown\");\n   287→                transactionManager.close();\n   288→            }\n   289→            log.debug(\"Aborting incomplete batches due to forced shutdown\");\n   290→            this.accumulator.abortIncompleteBatches();\n   291→        }\n   292→        try {\n   293→            this.client.close();\n   294→        } catch (Exception e) {\n   295→            log.error(\"Failed to close network client\", e);\n   296→        }\n   297→\n   298→        log.debug(\"Shutdown of Kafka producer I/O thread has completed.\");\n   299→    }\n   300→\n   301→    /**\n   302→     * Run a single iteration of sending\n   303→     *\n   304→     */\n   305→    void runOnce() {\n   306→        if (transactionManager != null) {\n   307→            try {\n   308→                transactionManager.maybeResolveSequences();\n   309→\n   310→                RuntimeException lastError = transactionManager.lastError();\n   311→\n   312→                // do not continue sending if the transaction manager is in a failed state\n   313→                if (transactionManager.hasFatalError()) {\n   314→                    if (lastError != null)\n   315→                        maybeAbortBatches(lastError);\n   316→                    client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n   317→                    return;\n   318→                }\n   319→\n   320→                if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError() && shouldHandleAuthorizationError(lastError)) {\n   321→                    return;\n   322→                }\n   323→\n   324→                // Check whether we need a new producerId. If so, we will enqueue an InitProducerId\n   325→                // request which will be sent below\n   326→                transactionManager.bumpIdempotentEpochAndResetIdIfNeeded();\n   327→\n   328→                if (maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest()) {\n   329→                    return;\n   330→                }\n   331→            } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n   332→                // This is already logged as error, but propagated here to perform any clean ups.\n   333→                log.trace(\"Authentication exception while processing transactional request\", e);\n   334→                transactionManager.authenticationFailed(e);\n   335→            }\n   336→        }\n   337→\n   338→        long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n   339→        long pollTimeout = sendProducerData(currentTimeMs);\n   340→        client.poll(pollTimeout, currentTimeMs);\n   341→    }\n   342→\n   343→    // We handle {@code TransactionalIdAuthorizationException} and {@code ClusterAuthorizationException} by first\n   344→    // failing the inflight requests, then transition the state to UNINITIALIZED so that the user doesn't need to\n   345→    // instantiate the producer again.\n   346→    private boolean shouldHandleAuthorizationError(RuntimeException exception) {\n   347→        if (exception instanceof TransactionalIdAuthorizationException ||\n   348→                        exception instanceof ClusterAuthorizationException) {\n   349→            transactionManager.failPendingRequests(new AuthenticationException(exception));\n   350→            maybeAbortBatches(exception);\n   351→            transactionManager.transitionToUninitialized(exception);\n   352→            return true;\n   353→        }\n   354→        return false;\n   355→    }\n   356→\n   357→    private long sendProducerData(long now) {\n   358→        MetadataSnapshot metadataSnapshot = metadata.fetchMetadataSnapshot();\n   359→        // get the list of partitions with data ready to send\n   360→        RecordAccumulator.ReadyCheckResult result = this.accumulator.ready(metadataSnapshot, now);\n   361→\n   362→        // if there are any partitions whose leaders are not known yet, force metadata update\n   363→        if (!result.unknownLeaderTopics.isEmpty()) {\n   364→            // The set of topics with unknown leader contains topics with leader election pending as well as\n   365→            // topics which may have expired. Add the topic again to metadata to ensure it is included\n   366→            // and request metadata update, since there are messages to send to the topic.\n   367→            for (String topic : result.unknownLeaderTopics)\n   368→                this.metadata.add(topic, now);\n   369→\n   370→            log.debug(\"Requesting metadata update due to unknown leader topics from the batched records: {}\",\n   371→                result.unknownLeaderTopics);\n   372→            this.metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n   373→        }\n   374→\n   375→        // remove any nodes we aren't ready to send to\n   376→        Iterator<Node> iter = result.readyNodes.iterator();\n   377→        long notReadyTimeout = Long.MAX_VALUE;\n   378→        while (iter.hasNext()) {\n   379→            Node node = iter.next();\n   380→            if (!this.client.ready(node, now)) {\n   381→                // Update just the readyTimeMs of the latency stats, so that it moves forward\n   382→                // every time the batch is ready (then the difference between readyTimeMs and\n   383→                // drainTimeMs would represent how long data is waiting for the node).\n   384→                this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, false);\n   385→                iter.remove();\n   386→                notReadyTimeout = Math.min(notReadyTimeout, this.client.pollDelayMs(node, now));\n   387→            } else {\n   388→                // Update both readyTimeMs and drainTimeMs, this would \"reset\" the node\n   389→                // latency.\n   390→                this.accumulator.updateNodeLatencyStats(node.id(), now, true);\n   391→            }\n   392→        }\n   393→\n   394→        // create produce requests\n   395→        Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> batches = this.accumulator.drain(metadataSnapshot, result.readyNodes, this.maxRequestSize, now);\n   396→        addToInflightBatches(batches);\n   397→        if (guaranteeMessageOrder) {\n   398→            // Mute all the partitions drained\n   399→            for (List<ProducerBatch> batchList : batches.values()) {\n   400→                for (ProducerBatch batch : batchList)\n   401→                    this.accumulator.mutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n   402→            }\n   403→        }\n   404→\n   405→        accumulator.resetNextBatchExpiryTime();\n   406→        List<ProducerBatch> expiredInflightBatches = getExpiredInflightBatches(now);\n   407→        List<ProducerBatch> expiredBatches = this.accumulator.expiredBatches(now);\n   408→        expiredBatches.addAll(expiredInflightBatches);\n   409→\n   410→        // Reset the producer id if an expired batch has previously been sent to the broker. Also update the metrics\n   411→        // for expired batches. see the documentation of @TransactionState.resetIdempotentProducerId to understand why\n   412→        // we need to reset the producer id here.\n   413→        if (!expiredBatches.isEmpty())\n   414→            log.trace(\"Expired {} batches in accumulator\", expiredBatches.size());\n   415→        for (ProducerBatch expiredBatch : expiredBatches) {\n   416→            String errorMessage = \"Expiring \" + expiredBatch.recordCount + \" record(s) for \" + expiredBatch.topicPartition\n   417→                + \":\" + (now - expiredBatch.createdMs) + \" ms has passed since batch creation\";\n   418→            failBatch(expiredBatch, new TimeoutException(errorMessage), false);\n   419→            if (transactionManager != null && expiredBatch.inRetry()) {\n   420→                // This ensures that no new batches are drained until the current in flight batches are fully resolved.\n   421→                transactionManager.markSequenceUnresolved(expiredBatch);\n   422→            }\n   423→        }\n   424→        sensors.updateProduceRequestMetrics(batches);\n   425→\n   426→        // If we have any nodes that are ready to send + have sendable data, poll with 0 timeout so this can immediately\n   427→        // loop and try sending more data. Otherwise, the timeout will be the smaller value between next batch expiry\n   428→        // time, and the delay time for checking data availability. Note that the nodes may have data that isn't yet\n   429→        // sendable due to lingering, backing off, etc. This specifically does not include nodes with sendable data\n   430→        // that aren't ready to send since they would cause busy looping.\n   431→        long pollTimeout = Math.min(result.nextReadyCheckDelayMs, notReadyTimeout);\n   432→        pollTimeout = Math.min(pollTimeout, this.accumulator.nextExpiryTimeMs() - now);\n   433→        pollTimeout = Math.max(pollTimeout, 0);\n   434→        if (!result.readyNodes.isEmpty()) {\n   435→            log.trace(\"Nodes with data ready to send: {}\", result.readyNodes);\n   436→            // if some partitions are already ready to be sent, the select time would be 0;\n   437→            // otherwise if some partition already has some data accumulated but not ready yet,\n   438→            // the select time will be the time difference between now and its linger expiry time;\n   439→            // otherwise the select time will be the time difference between now and the metadata expiry time;\n   440→            pollTimeout = 0;\n   441→        }\n   442→        sendProduceRequests(batches, now);\n   443→        return pollTimeout;\n   444→    }\n   445→\n   446→    /**\n   447→     * Returns true if a transactional request is sent or polled, or if a FindCoordinator request is enqueued\n   448→     */\n   449→    private boolean maybeSendAndPollTransactionalRequest() {\n   450→        if (transactionManager.hasInFlightRequest()) {\n   451→            // as long as there are outstanding transactional requests, we simply wait for them to return\n   452→            client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n   453→            return true;\n   454→        }\n   455→\n   456→        if (transactionManager.hasAbortableError()) {\n   457→            accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(transactionManager.lastError());\n   458→        } else if (transactionManager.isAborting()) {\n   459→            accumulator.abortUndrainedBatches(new TransactionAbortedException());\n   460→        }\n   461→\n   462→        TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler = transactionManager.nextRequest(accumulator.hasIncomplete());\n   463→        if (nextRequestHandler == null)\n   464→            return false;\n   465→\n   466→        AbstractRequest.Builder<?> requestBuilder = nextRequestHandler.requestBuilder();\n   467→        Node targetNode = null;\n   468→        try {\n   469→            FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType = nextRequestHandler.coordinatorType();\n   470→            targetNode = coordinatorType != null ?\n   471→                    transactionManager.coordinator(coordinatorType) :\n   472→                    client.leastLoadedNode(time.milliseconds()).node();\n   473→            if (targetNode != null) {\n   474→                if (!awaitNodeReady(targetNode, coordinatorType)) {\n   475→                    log.trace(\"Target node {} not ready within request timeout, will retry when node is ready.\", targetNode);\n   476→                    maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n   477→                    return true;\n   478→                }\n   479→            } else if (coordinatorType != null) {\n   480→                log.trace(\"Coordinator not known for {}, will retry {} after finding coordinator.\", coordinatorType, requestBuilder.apiKey());\n   481→                maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n   482→                return true;\n   483→            } else {\n   484→                log.trace(\"No nodes available to send requests, will poll and retry when until a node is ready.\");\n   485→                transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n   486→                client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n   487→                return true;\n   488→            }\n   489→\n   490→            if (nextRequestHandler.isRetry())\n   491→                time.sleep(nextRequestHandler.retryBackoffMs());\n   492→\n   493→            long currentTimeMs = time.milliseconds();\n   494→            ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(targetNode.idString(), requestBuilder, currentTimeMs,\n   495→                true, requestTimeoutMs, nextRequestHandler);\n   496→            log.debug(\"Sending transactional request {} to node {} with correlation ID {}\", requestBuilder, targetNode, clientRequest.correlationId());\n   497→            client.send(clientRequest, currentTimeMs);\n   498→            transactionManager.setInFlightCorrelationId(clientRequest.correlationId());\n   499→            client.poll(retryBackoffMs, time.milliseconds());\n   500→            return true;\n   501→        } catch (IOException e) {\n   502→            log.debug(\"Disconnect from {} while trying to send request {}. Going \" +\n   503→                    \"to back off and retry.\", targetNode, requestBuilder, e);\n   504→            // We break here so that we pick up the FindCoordinator request immediately.\n   505→            maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(nextRequestHandler);\n   506→            return true;\n   507→        }\n   508→    }\n   509→\n   510→    private void maybeFindCoordinatorAndRetry(TransactionManager.TxnRequestHandler nextRequestHandler) {\n   511→        if (nextRequestHandler.needsCoordinator()) {\n   512→            transactionManager.lookupCoordinator(nextRequestHandler);\n   513→        } else {\n   514→            // For non-coordinator requests, sleep here to prevent a tight loop when no node is available\n   515→            time.sleep(retryBackoffMs);\n   516→            metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n   517→        }\n   518→\n   519→        transactionManager.retry(nextRequestHandler);\n   520→    }\n   521→\n   522→    private void maybeAbortBatches(RuntimeException exception) {\n   523→        if (accumulator.hasIncomplete()) {\n   524→            log.error(\"Aborting producer batches due to fatal error\", exception);\n   525→            accumulator.abortBatches(exception);\n   526→        }\n   527→    }\n   528→\n   529→    /**\n   530→     * Start closing the sender (won't actually complete until all data is sent out)\n   531→     */\n   532→    public void initiateClose() {\n   533→        // Ensure accumulator is closed first to guarantee that no more appends are accepted after\n   534→        // breaking from the sender loop. Otherwise, we may miss some callbacks when shutting down.\n   535→        this.accumulator.close();\n   536→        this.running = false;\n   537→        this.wakeup();\n   538→    }\n   539→\n   540→    /**\n   541→     * Closes the sender without sending out any pending messages.\n   542→     */\n   543→    public void forceClose() {\n   544→        this.forceClose = true;\n   545→        initiateClose();\n   546→    }\n   547→\n   548→    public boolean isRunning() {\n   549→        return running;\n   550→    }\n   551→\n   552→    private boolean awaitNodeReady(Node node, FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType coordinatorType) throws IOException {\n   553→        if (NetworkClientUtils.awaitReady(client, node, time, requestTimeoutMs)) {\n   554→            if (coordinatorType == FindCoordinatorRequest.CoordinatorType.TRANSACTION) {\n   555→                // Indicate to the transaction manager that the coordinator is ready, allowing it to check ApiVersions\n   556→                // This allows us to bump transactional epochs even if the coordinator is temporarily unavailable at\n   557→                // the time when the abortable error is handled\n   558→                transactionManager.handleCoordinatorReady();\n   559→            }\n   560→            return true;\n   561→        }\n   562→        return false;\n   563→    }\n   564→\n   565→    /**\n   566→     * Handle a produce response\n   567→     */\n   568→    private void handleProduceResponse(ClientResponse response, Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> batches, Map<Uuid, String> topicNames, long now) {\n   569→        RequestHeader requestHeader = response.requestHeader();\n   570→        int correlationId = requestHeader.correlationId();\n   571→        if (response.wasTimedOut()) {\n   572→            log.trace(\"Cancelled request with header {} due to the last request to node {} timed out\",\n   573→                requestHeader, response.destination());\n   574→            for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n   575→                completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.REQUEST_TIMED_OUT, String.format(\"Disconnected from node %s due to timeout\", response.destination())),\n   576→                        correlationId, now, null);\n   577→        } else if (response.wasDisconnected()) {\n   578→            log.trace(\"Cancelled request with header {} due to node {} being disconnected\",\n   579→                requestHeader, response.destination());\n   580→            for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n   581→                completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NETWORK_EXCEPTION, String.format(\"Disconnected from node %s\", response.destination())),\n   582→                        correlationId, now, null);\n   583→        } else if (response.versionMismatch() != null) {\n   584→            log.warn(\"Cancelled request {} due to a version mismatch with node {}\",\n   585→                    response, response.destination(), response.versionMismatch());\n   586→            for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values())\n   587→                completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION), correlationId, now, null);\n   588→        } else {\n   589→            log.trace(\"Received produce response from node {} with correlation id {}\", response.destination(), correlationId);\n   590→            // if we have a response, parse it\n   591→            if (response.hasResponse()) {\n   592→                // Sender should exercise PartitionProduceResponse rather than ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse\n   593→                // https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/KAFKA-10696\n   594→                ProduceResponse produceResponse = (ProduceResponse) response.responseBody();\n   595→                // This will be set by completeBatch.\n   596→                Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo = new HashMap<>();\n   597→                produceResponse.data().responses().forEach(r -> r.partitionResponses().forEach(p -> {\n   598→                    ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse partResp = new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(\n   599→                            Errors.forCode(p.errorCode()),\n   600→                            p.baseOffset(),\n   601→                            p.logAppendTimeMs(),\n   602→                            p.logStartOffset(),\n   603→                            p.recordErrors()\n   604→                                .stream()\n   605→                                .map(e -> new ProduceResponse.RecordError(e.batchIndex(), e.batchIndexErrorMessage()))\n   606→                                .collect(Collectors.toList()),\n   607→                            p.errorMessage(),\n   608→                            p.currentLeader());\n   609→\n   610→                    // Version 13 drop topic name and add support to topic id.\n   611→                    // We need to find batch based on topic id and partition index only as\n   612→                    // topic name in the response will be empty.\n   613→                    // For older versions, topic id is zero, and we will find the batch based on the topic name.\n   614→                    TopicPartition tp = (!r.topicId().equals(Uuid.ZERO_UUID) && topicNames.containsKey(r.topicId())) ?\n   615→                            new TopicPartition(topicNames.get(r.topicId()), p.index()) :\n   616→                            new TopicPartition(r.name(), p.index());\n   617→\n   618→                    ProducerBatch batch = batches.get(tp);\n   619→                    if (batch == null) {\n   620→                        throw new IllegalStateException(\"Can't find batch created for topic id \" + r.topicId() +\n   621→                                \" topic name \" + r.name() + \" partition \" + p.index() + \" using \" + topicNames);\n   622→                    }\n   623→                    completeBatch(batch, partResp, correlationId, now, partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo);\n   624→                }));\n   625→\n   626→                if (!partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.isEmpty()) {\n   627→                    List<Node> leaderNodes = produceResponse.data().nodeEndpoints().stream()\n   628→                        .map(e -> new Node(e.nodeId(), e.host(), e.port(), e.rack()))\n   629→                        .filter(e -> !e.equals(Node.noNode()))\n   630→                        .collect(\n   631→                            Collectors.toList());\n   632→                    Set<TopicPartition> updatedPartitions = metadata.updatePartitionLeadership(partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo, leaderNodes);\n   633→                    if (log.isTraceEnabled()) {\n   634→                        updatedPartitions.forEach(\n   635→                            part -> log.debug(\"For {} leader was updated.\", part)\n   636→                        );\n   637→                    }\n   638→                }\n   639→\n   640→                this.sensors.recordLatency(response.destination(), response.requestLatencyMs());\n   641→            } else {\n   642→                // this is the acks = 0 case, just complete all requests\n   643→                for (ProducerBatch batch : batches.values()) {\n   644→                    completeBatch(batch, new ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse(Errors.NONE), correlationId, now, null);\n   645→                }\n   646→            }\n   647→        }\n   648→    }\n   649→\n   650→    /**\n   651→     * Complete or retry the given batch of records.\n   652→     *\n   653→     * @param batch The record batch\n   654→     * @param response The produce response\n   655→     * @param correlationId The correlation id for the request\n   656→     * @param now The current POSIX timestamp in milliseconds\n   657→     * @param partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo This will be populated with partitions that have updated leader info.\n   658→     */\n   659→    private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long correlationId,\n   660→                               long now, Map<TopicPartition, Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch> partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo) {\n   661→        Errors error = response.error;\n   662→\n   663→        if (error == Errors.MESSAGE_TOO_LARGE && batch.recordCount > 1 && !batch.isDone() &&\n   664→                (batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 || batch.isCompressed())) {\n   665→            // If the batch is too large, we split the batch and send the split batches again. We do not decrement\n   666→            // the retry attempts in this case.\n   667→            log.warn(\n   668→                \"Got error produce response in correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, splitting and retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n   669→                correlationId,\n   670→                batch.topicPartition,\n   671→                this.retries - batch.attempts(),\n   672→                formatErrMsg(response));\n   673→            if (transactionManager != null)\n   674→                transactionManager.removeInFlightBatch(batch);\n   675→            this.accumulator.splitAndReenqueue(batch);\n   676→            maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n   677→            this.sensors.recordBatchSplit();\n   678→        } else if (error != Errors.NONE) {\n   679→            if (canRetry(batch, response, now)) {\n   680→                log.warn(\n   681→                    \"Got error produce response with correlation id {} on topic-partition {}, retrying ({} attempts left). Error: {}\",\n   682→                    correlationId,\n   683→                    batch.topicPartition,\n   684→                    this.retries - batch.attempts() - 1,\n   685→                    formatErrMsg(response));\n   686→                reenqueueBatch(batch, now);\n   687→            } else if (error == Errors.DUPLICATE_SEQUENCE_NUMBER) {\n   688→                // If we have received a duplicate sequence error, it means that the sequence number has advanced beyond\n   689→                // the sequence of the current batch, and we haven't retained batch metadata on the broker to return\n   690→                // the correct offset and timestamp.\n   691→                //\n   692→                // The only thing we can do is to return success to the user and not return a valid offset and timestamp.\n   693→                completeBatch(batch, response);\n   694→            } else {\n   695→                // tell the user the result of their request. We only adjust sequence numbers if the batch didn't exhaust\n   696→                // its retries -- if it did, we don't know whether the sequence number was accepted or not, and\n   697→                // thus it is not safe to reassign the sequence.\n   698→                failBatch(batch, response, batch.attempts() < this.retries);\n   699→            }\n   700→            if (error.exception() instanceof InvalidMetadataException) {\n   701→                if (error.exception() instanceof UnknownTopicOrPartitionException) {\n   702→                    log.warn(\"Received unknown topic or partition error in produce request on partition {}. The \" +\n   703→                            \"topic-partition may not exist or the user may not have Describe access to it\",\n   704→                        batch.topicPartition);\n   705→                } else {\n   706→                    log.warn(\"Received invalid metadata error in produce request on partition {} due to {} Going \" +\n   707→                            \"to request metadata update now\", batch.topicPartition, error.exception(response.errorMessage).toString());\n   708→                }\n   709→                if (error.exception() instanceof NotLeaderOrFollowerException || error.exception() instanceof FencedLeaderEpochException) {\n   710→                    log.debug(\"For {}, received error {}, with leaderIdAndEpoch {}\", batch.topicPartition, error, response.currentLeader);\n   711→                    if (partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo != null\n   712→                        && (response.currentLeader.leaderId() != -1 && response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch() != -1)) {\n   713→                        partitionsWithUpdatedLeaderInfo.put(batch.topicPartition, new Metadata.LeaderIdAndEpoch(\n   714→                            Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderId()), Optional.of(response.currentLeader.leaderEpoch())));\n   715→                    }\n   716→                }\n   717→                metadata.requestUpdate(false);\n   718→            }\n   719→        } else {\n   720→            completeBatch(batch, response);\n   721→        }\n   722→\n   723→        // Unmute the completed partition.\n   724→        if (guaranteeMessageOrder)\n   725→            this.accumulator.unmutePartition(batch.topicPartition);\n   726→    }\n   727→\n   728→    /**\n   729→     * Format the error from a {@link ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse} in a user-friendly string\n   730→     * e.g \"NETWORK_EXCEPTION. Error Message: Disconnected from node 0\"\n   731→     */\n   732→    private String formatErrMsg(ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n   733→        String errorMessageSuffix = (response.errorMessage == null || response.errorMessage.isEmpty()) ?\n   734→                \"\" : String.format(\". Error Message: %s\", response.errorMessage);\n   735→        return String.format(\"%s%s\", response.error, errorMessageSuffix);\n   736→    }\n   737→\n   738→    private void reenqueueBatch(ProducerBatch batch, long currentTimeMs) {\n   739→        this.accumulator.reenqueue(batch, currentTimeMs);\n   740→        maybeRemoveFromInflightBatches(batch);\n   741→        this.sensors.recordRetries(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\n   742→    }\n   743→\n   744→    private void completeBatch(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response) {\n   745→        if (transactionManager != null) {\n   746→            transactionManager.handleCompletedBatch(batch, response);\n   747→        }\n   748→\n   749→        if (batch.complete(response.baseOffset, response.logAppendTime)) {\n   750→            maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n   751→        }\n   752→    }\n   753→\n   754→    private void failBatch(ProducerBatch batch,\n   755→                           ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response,\n   756→                           boolean adjustSequenceNumbers) {\n   757→        final RuntimeException topLevelException;\n   758→        if (response.error == Errors.TOPIC_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\n   759→            topLevelException = new TopicAuthorizationException(Collections.singleton(batch.topicPartition.topic()));\n   760→        else if (response.error == Errors.CLUSTER_AUTHORIZATION_FAILED)\n   761→            topLevelException = new ClusterAuthorizationException(\"The producer is not authorized to do idempotent sends\");\n   762→        else\n   763→            topLevelException = response.error.exception(response.errorMessage);\n   764→\n   765→        if (response.recordErrors == null || response.recordErrors.isEmpty()) {\n   766→            failBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n   767→        } else {\n   768→            Map<Integer, RuntimeException> recordErrorMap = new HashMap<>(response.recordErrors.size());\n   769→            for (ProduceResponse.RecordError recordError : response.recordErrors) {\n   770→                // The API leaves us with some awkwardness interpreting the errors in the response.\n   771→                // We cannot differentiate between different error cases (such as INVALID_TIMESTAMP)\n   772→                // from the single error code at the partition level, so instead we use INVALID_RECORD\n   773→                // for all failed records and rely on the message to distinguish the cases.\n   774→                final String errorMessage;\n   775→                if (recordError.message != null) {\n   776→                    errorMessage = recordError.message;\n   777→                } else if (response.errorMessage != null) {\n   778→                    errorMessage = response.errorMessage;\n   779→                } else {\n   780→                    errorMessage = response.error.message();\n   781→                }\n   782→\n   783→                // If the batch contained only a single record error, then we can unambiguously\n   784→                // use the exception type corresponding to the partition-level error code.\n   785→                if (response.recordErrors.size() == 1) {\n   786→                    recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, response.error.exception(errorMessage));\n   787→                } else {\n   788→                    recordErrorMap.put(recordError.batchIndex, new InvalidRecordException(errorMessage));\n   789→                }\n   790→            }\n   791→\n   792→            Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions = batchIndex -> {\n   793→                RuntimeException exception = recordErrorMap.get(batchIndex);\n   794→                if (exception != null) {\n   795→                    return exception;\n   796→                } else {\n   797→                    // If the response contains record errors, then the records which failed validation\n   798→                    // will be present in the response. To avoid confusion for the remaining records, we\n   799→                    // return a generic exception.\n   800→                    return new KafkaException(\"Failed to append record because it was part of a batch \" +\n   801→                        \"which had one more more invalid records\");\n   802→                }\n   803→            };\n   804→\n   805→            failBatch(batch, topLevelException, recordExceptions, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n   806→        }\n   807→    }\n   808→\n   809→    private void failBatch(\n   810→        ProducerBatch batch,\n   811→        RuntimeException topLevelException,\n   812→        boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\n   813→    ) {\n   814→        failBatch(batch, topLevelException, batchIndex -> topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n   815→    }\n   816→\n   817→    private void failBatch(\n   818→        ProducerBatch batch,\n   819→        RuntimeException topLevelException,\n   820→        Function<Integer, RuntimeException> recordExceptions,\n   821→        boolean adjustSequenceNumbers\n   822→    ) {\n   823→        this.sensors.recordErrors(batch.topicPartition.topic(), batch.recordCount);\n   824→\n   825→        if (batch.completeExceptionally(topLevelException, recordExceptions)) {\n   826→            if (transactionManager != null) {\n   827→                try {\n   828→                    // This call can throw an exception in the rare case that there's an invalid state transition\n   829→                    // attempted. Catch these so as not to interfere with the rest of the logic.\n   830→                    transactionManager.handleFailedBatch(batch, topLevelException, adjustSequenceNumbers);\n   831→                } catch (Exception e) {\n   832→                    log.debug(\"Encountered error when transaction manager was handling a failed batch\", e);\n   833→                }\n   834→            }\n   835→            maybeRemoveAndDeallocateBatch(batch);\n   836→        }\n   837→    }\n   838→\n   839→    /**\n   840→     * We can retry a send if the error is transient and the number of attempts taken is fewer than the maximum allowed.\n   841→     * We can also retry OutOfOrderSequence exceptions for future batches, since if the first batch has failed, the\n   842→     * future batches are certain to fail with an OutOfOrderSequence exception.\n   843→     */\n   844→    private boolean canRetry(ProducerBatch batch, ProduceResponse.PartitionResponse response, long now) {\n   845→        return !batch.hasReachedDeliveryTimeout(accumulator.getDeliveryTimeoutMs(), now) &&\n   846→            batch.attempts() < this.retries &&\n   847→            !batch.isDone() &&\n   848→            (transactionManager == null ?\n   849→                    response.error.exception() instanceof RetriableException :\n   850→                    transactionManager.canRetry(response, batch));\n   851→    }\n   852→\n   853→    /**\n   854→     * Transfer the record batches into a list of produce requests on a per-node basis\n   855→     */\n   856→    private void sendProduceRequests(Map<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> collated, long now) {\n   857→        for (Map.Entry<Integer, List<ProducerBatch>> entry : collated.entrySet())\n   858→            sendProduceRequest(now, entry.getKey(), acks, requestTimeoutMs, entry.getValue());\n   859→    }\n   860→\n   861→    /**\n   862→     * Create a produce request from the given record batches\n   863→     */\n   864→    private void sendProduceRequest(long now, int destination, short acks, int timeout, List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\n   865→        if (batches.isEmpty())\n   866→            return;\n   867→\n   868→        final Map<TopicPartition, ProducerBatch> recordsByPartition = new HashMap<>(batches.size());\n   869→        Map<String, Uuid> topicIds = topicIdsForBatches(batches);\n   870→\n   871→        ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection tpd = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceDataCollection();\n   872→        for (ProducerBatch batch : batches) {\n   873→            TopicPartition tp = batch.topicPartition;\n   874→            MemoryRecords records = batch.records();\n   875→            Uuid topicId = topicIds.get(tp.topic());\n   876→            ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData tpData = tpd.find(tp.topic(), topicId);\n   877→\n   878→            if (tpData == null) {\n   879→                tpData = new ProduceRequestData.TopicProduceData()\n   880→                        .setTopicId(topicId).setName(tp.topic());\n   881→                tpd.add(tpData);\n   882→            }\n   883→\n   884→            tpData.partitionData().add(new ProduceRequestData.PartitionProduceData()\n   885→                    .setIndex(tp.partition())\n   886→                    .setRecords(records));\n   887→            recordsByPartition.put(tp, batch);\n   888→        }\n   889→\n   890→        String transactionalId = null;\n   891→        boolean useTransactionV1Version = false;\n   892→        if (transactionManager != null && transactionManager.isTransactional()) {\n   893→            transactionalId = transactionManager.transactionalId();\n   894→            useTransactionV1Version = !transactionManager.isTransactionV2Enabled();\n   895→        }\n   896→\n   897→        ProduceRequest.Builder requestBuilder = ProduceRequest.builder(\n   898→                new ProduceRequestData()\n   899→                        .setAcks(acks)\n   900→                        .setTimeoutMs(timeout)\n   901→                        .setTransactionalId(transactionalId)\n   902→                        .setTopicData(tpd),\n   903→                useTransactionV1Version\n   904→        );\n   905→        // Fetch topic names from metadata outside callback as topic ids may change during the callback\n   906→        // for example if topic was recreated.\n   907→        Map<Uuid, String> topicNames = metadata.topicNames();\n   908→\n   909→        RequestCompletionHandler callback = response -> handleProduceResponse(response, recordsByPartition, topicNames, time.milliseconds());\n   910→\n   911→        String nodeId = Integer.toString(destination);\n   912→        ClientRequest clientRequest = client.newClientRequest(nodeId, requestBuilder, now, acks != 0,\n   913→                requestTimeoutMs, callback);\n   914→        client.send(clientRequest, now);\n   915→        log.trace(\"Sent produce request to {}: {}\", nodeId, requestBuilder);\n   916→    }\n   917→\n   918→    private Map<String, Uuid> topicIdsForBatches(List<ProducerBatch> batches) {\n   919→        return batches.stream()\n   920→                .collect(Collectors.toMap(\n   921→                        b -> b.topicPartition.topic(),\n   922→                        b -> metadata.topicIds().getOrDefault(b.topicPartition.topic(), Uuid.ZERO_UUID),\n   923→                        (existing, replacement) -> replacement)\n   924→                );\n   925→    }\n   926→\n   927→    /**\n   928→     * Wake up the selector associated with this send thread\n   929→     */\n   930→    public void wakeup() {\n   931→        this.client.wakeup();\n   932→    }\n   933→\n   934→    public static Sensor throttleTimeSensor(SenderMetricsRegistry metrics) {\n   935→        Sensor produceThrottleTimeSensor =           long now = time.milliseconds();\n  1038→            for (List<ProducerBatch> nodeBatch : batches.values()) {\n  1039→                int records = 0;\n  1040→                for     if (callbacks != null)\n            callbacks.setPartition(partition);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Check if partition concurrently changed, or we need to complete previously disabled partition change.\n     *\n     * @param topic The topic\n     * @param topicInfo The topic info\n     * @param partitionInfo The built-in partitioner's partition info\n     * @param deque The partition queue\n     * @param nowMs The current time, in milliseconds\n     * @param cluster THe cluster metadata\n     * @return 'true' if partition changed and we need to get new partition info and retry,\n     *         'false' otherwise\n     */\n    private boolean partitionChanged(String topic,\n                                     TopicInfo topicInfo,\n                                     BuiltInPartitioner.StickyPartitionInfo partitionInfo,\n                                     Deque<ProducerBatch> deque, long nowMs,\n                                     Cluster cluster) {\n        if (topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.isPartitionChanged(partitionInfo)) {\n            log.trace(\"Partition {} for topic {} switched by a concurrent append, retrying\",\n                    partitionInfo.partition(), topic);\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        // We might have disabled partition switch if the queue had incomplete batches.\n        // Check if all batches are full now and switch .\n        if (allBatchesFull(deque)) {\n            topicInfo.builtInPartitioner.updatePartitionInfo(partitionInfo, 0, cluster, true);\n            if topic, partitionInfo.partition());\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Add a record to the accumulator, return the append         long timestamp,\n                                     byte[] key,\n                                     byte[] value,\n                                     Header[] headers,\n                                     AppendCallbacks callbacks,\n                                     long maxTimeToBlock,\n                                     long nowMs,\n                                     Cluster
